# KEY-AUDIT-2026-07-19 — touch-drag viability + answer-key accuracy (Grade 4)

Executed per `BRIEF-AUDIT-KEYS.md`, 2026-07-20 (session started 2026-07-19 IST window). READ-ONLY: no lesson,
engine, or tool file was modified; all working scripts are new untracked files under `tools/scratch/`.

## Opening summary (mandatory)

The Grade-4 corpus in `lessons/` measures **3075 questions in 118 lesson files** — exactly the recorded
3,075, no difference to enumerate. Of these, **516 questions (16.8%) were CHECKABLE** —
a machine derived the correct answer from the question's own data and compared it with the stamped key —
and **2559 (83.2%) were NOT CHECKABLE** by this audit. Checks B1–B3 ran on the
checkable subset; structural check B4 and enrichment check B5 ran on ALL 3075 questions.
**Defects found: 0.** The checking machinery is proven live: 156 deliberately mutated keys across
113 solver families were all flagged, and Q19 re-keyed to "B" is flagged by B3 (see Phase B).

**What this audit does NOT cover, stated plainly: the 2,559 NOT-CHECKABLE questions (83.2% of the corpus)
were not verified for answer-key accuracy beyond structural checks (B4) and enrichment-consistency checks (B5).
Nothing was learned about whether their keys are arithmetically right. A clean result on the 516 checkable
questions is NOT a clean bill of health for the corpus.** An unknown is reported as an unknown — the full
per-question UNVERIFIABLE table is at the end of this report.

**Phase 0 headline:** all three in-repo drag paths (order/sequence-build tile drag, categorize tile drag)
PASS all four steps under real CDP touch emulation at 390px — a child on a phone can answer those 338
questions today. The `construct` path (31 questions) is **UNVERIFIED — its geometry engine (`raoGeoEngine.js`)
is not in this repository** (review pages render 'Geometry engine not loaded'). The ruler-slide path exists
in the engine but no Grade-4 question uses it. The known Q19 defect **is not present in the current tree**
(stamped key is A, which is correct) — a finding that contradicts the brief's premise; evidence in Phase B.

---

## Phase 0 — touch-drag viability

### 0.1 Drag paths discovered (from the engine, not from assumption)

| # | path | entry function | binds at | events bound |
|---|------|----------------|----------|--------------|
| P1 | order / sequence-build tile drag | `enableTileDrag()` — `engine/preview-engine.js:2018` | `root pointerdown` :2100; window `pointermove`/`pointerup`/`pointercancel` :2032–2034; slot-tap `click` :2101 | Pointer events |
| P2 | categorize tile drag | inline in `categorize.bind()` — `engine/preview-engine.js:2365` | `root pointerdown` :2378; window move/up/cancel :2371 | Pointer events |
| P3 | ruler slide (measure-drag) | `enableRulerSlide()` — `engine/preview-engine.js:2106` | `svg pointerdown` :2132 | Pointer events; sets `touchAction="none"` inline :2131 |
| P4 | construct geometry | `construct.bind()` → `window.RaoGeo.mount` — `engine/preview-engine.js:2394–2401` | **not in this repo** (`raoGeoEngine.js` is app-side; only a test stub exists at `tools/verify-reset.js:61`) | UNKNOWN — cannot be read here |

**The chat's working assumption (two paths) is contradicted: there are three in-repo pointer-event paths**
**plus one external (construct).** P1 serves two behaviors (order and sequence-build) through one function.
Additionally, `sequence-build` has a tap-only `pat-strip` variant and `line-plot` is click-based — taps, not drags.

**HTML5 drag-and-drop: not used.** Tiles carry vestigial `draggable="true"` attributes
(engine lines 1033/1704/1731) but no `dragstart`/`dragover`/`drop` handler exists anywhere in the engine —
nothing relies on the API that is dead on touch devices. All real dragging is pointer-event based, which fires
on touch *provided* `touch-action` permits it: `rao.css:611` supplies `touch-action:none` for
`.tile, .vs-tile, .order-slot, .sb-tile` (plus `rao.css:219` for `.tile`). Phase 0.4 proves this rule is load-bearing.

### 0.2 Exposure — the blast radius

| path | questions |
|------|-----------|
| P1 order (`.tile` → `.order-slot`) | 153 |
| P1 sequence-build (`.sb-tile` → `.sb-slot`) | 31 |
| P2 categorize (`.vs-tile` → zones/bins/venn) | 154 |
| P3 ruler slide | 0 — no Grade-4 question uses it |
| P4 construct | 31 (30 in real lessons + 1 in the `_type-coverage` fixture) |
| **total drag-dependent** | **369** |

Plainly: **338 questions depend on the two tile-drag paths** — if either of those
paths were dead on phones, those questions would be unanswerable there; **31 more** depend on an engine
this repo cannot test.

### 0.3 Real-touch test — 390×800, CDP `Input.dispatchTouchEvent`

Harness: `tools/scratch/touch-drag-test.js` (new, untracked). Every drag is a raw CDP
`touchStart → 14 × touchMove → touchEnd` sequence — genuine touch events, NOT mouse events at a narrow
viewport. Test lesson: `lessons/compare_numbers_up_to_five_digits.html` (real corpus questions of all three
testable shapes). Every needed tile was dragged per the answer key, then the real Check button was tapped.

| path | 1. tile visibly moves (measured) | 2. lands in target | 3. registers in answer state (`serialize()`) | 4. Check grades CORRECT |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| P1 order | PASS — ghost delta dx=0, dy=−259.2px between move samples | PASS | PASS — `["15,234","15,243","15,324","15,423"]` | PASS — `raoOutcome=correct` |
| P1 sequence-build | PASS — ghost delta dx=−84, dy=−76px | PASS | PASS — `["9","7","4","3","1"]` | PASS — `raoOutcome=correct` (see Deviations: Check tap needed a re-tap before Chrome synthesized the click; the touch events themselves reached the button first time) |
| P2 categorize | PASS — ghost delta dx=74.8, dy=132.1px | PASS | PASS — `["under","over","under","over","over","under"]` | PASS — `raoOutcome=correct` |
| P3 ruler slide | N/A — zero exposure; no real Grade-4 question exists to test (brief requires a real question) | N/A | N/A | N/A |
| P4 construct | UNVERIFIED — `raoGeoEngine.js` not in this repository; nothing to load or drive | UNVERIFIED | UNVERIFIED | UNVERIFIED |

### 0.4 Sabotage proof — the harness observed failing

Sabotage was applied to an **in-memory copy** of the engine/CSS bytes injected into the test page; the files
on disk were never written. Two independent sabotages, each followed by a clean restore run:

**Sabotage A (`--sabotage=engine`)** — the injected engine copy ignores touch pointers in both tile paths.
Result: **12/12 checks FAIL** — for every path: `no drag ghost ever appeared (drag never started)`,
`serialize() = null`, and Check answers `✋ Answer it first` — the exact silent unanswerable-question failure
mode the brief describes.

**Sabotage B (`--sabotage=css`)** — the injected `rao.css` copy has both `touch-action:none` declarations
flipped to `auto` (the regression class fixed for `.sb-tile` in commit 2366311). Result: **12/12 checks FAIL**
with the same signature — proving under CDP touch emulation that `rao.css:611` is load-bearing: without it the
browser claims the gesture for scrolling and the drag never starts.

**Restore run** (no sabotage, pristine bytes): **13/13 PASS.** The harness therefore measures the DOM, and a
green run is a measurement, not faith.

`git status` at end of Phase 0, verbatim:

```
On branch main
Your branch is ahead of 'origin/main' by 6 commits.
  (use "git push" to publish your local commits)

Untracked files:
  (use "git add <file>..." to include in what will be committed)
	BRIEF-AUDIT-KEYS.md
	BRIEF-L1-ASMD.md
	BRIEF-RENDER-1.md
	review/__vf_Simple fractions - what fraction does the shape show.html
	tools/scratch/

nothing added to commit but untracked files present (use "git add" to track)
```

(The `review/__vf_…` file was created at 00:49 IST by a concurrent `verify-format` process from another
session — two unrelated `node.exe` processes were running. Not created and not touched by this audit; see Deviations.)

### 0.5 Phase 0 verdict, one sentence per path

- **P1 order / sequence-build:** a child on a phone can drag, drop, and be graded correctly today — measured, not assumed.
- **P2 categorize:** a child on a phone can drag tiles into bins/venn regions and be graded correctly today.
- **P3 ruler slide:** no Grade-4 question uses it, so no child is exposed; the path itself was not touch-tested.
- **P4 construct:** unknowable from this repository — 30 real questions ride on an engine that is not here, and that is itself a finding.

## Phase A — corpus partition

- Total questions measured: **3075** (recorded: 3,075 — **exact match**, nothing to reconcile). 118 files
  (117 lessons + the `_type-coverage.html` harness fixture, which lives in `lessons/` and is part of the recorded count).
- **CHECKABLE: 516 (16.8%)** — split by check family: B1: 487, B2: 17, B3: 12
- **NOT CHECKABLE: 2559 (83.2%)** — this is a headline number, not a footnote.

Checkable by question type: single-select: 204, fill-blanks: 148, order: 98, categorize: 26, multi-select: 20, time: 13, line-plot: 7

NOT-CHECKABLE reasons:

| reason | questions |
|---|---|
| prose-dependent (no computable pattern in prompt/options) | 1226 |
| prose-dependent word problem | 571 |
| figure-dependent (figure not machine-readable by this audit) | 477 |
| zone predicates not machine-computable | 128 |
| tiles/direction not machine-computable | 86 |
| construct self-grades — no key to audit | 31 |
| figure table not machine-readable | 25 |
| free-entry expression — answer restates prompt prose | 8 |
| bar-graph figure mapping not implemented | 3 |
| computed a quantity but options are prose — solver inapplicable | 2 |
| prose-dependent elapsed-time narrative | 1 |
| lattice digit-grid not implemented | 1 |

---

## Phase B — checks over the checkable bucket

Method: every solver computes the answer from the question's own data (prompt text, option values, tile
values, zone labels, SVG geometry) **before** the stamped key is read — solvers structurally cannot see the
key. Arithmetic in Python `Fraction`/`Decimal`; rounding is `ROUND_HALF_UP`. B4 (structural) and B5
(enrichment consistency) ran over the entire corpus, not just the checkable subset.

### Defect table

**0 defects found.** 
The table is empty. Per the brief's own standard, an empty table is only meaningful if the checks are
proven capable of firing — see the proof below.

### Proof the checks fire (`tools/scratch/selftest_mutations.py`)

- **156 stamped keys were mutated in memory** (wrong option, transposed order/categorize sequences, bumped
  fill values, wrong times) across **113 distinct solver families** covering B1, B2 and B3. **All 156 were
  flagged; 0 missed.**
- The B2 figure-vs-prompt contradiction check (which applies to exactly 2 questions — narrow reach, disclosed)
  was proven by perturbing a prompt dimension in memory: `prompt states 99×1 but the figure's dim labels read 3×4` → FLAGGED.

### Q19 — the question that commissioned this audit

**The audit's finding contradicts the brief's premise, and per the brief's own anti-laundering law this is
reported as a finding:** the brief states Q19's stamped key is **B** (wrong). In the current tree the stamped
key is **A** — in the lesson source (`lessons/incoming/area-and-perimeter-word-problems.html`), in the
generated `review/area-and-perimeter-word-problems.html` on disk, and the source file has exactly one commit
(`931352e`, its initial tracking) with no later amendment. B3 evaluates Q19 as: perimeter A = 2×(12+2) = **28 m**,
perimeter B = 2×(6+4) = **20 m**, comparison word **MORE** → correct answer **A** — which is what is stamped.
The question's own `explain` agrees ("A needs 28 m. B needs 20 m.").

To satisfy the brief's requirement that B3 must detect the Q19 pattern: Q19 was re-keyed to "B" **in memory**
and re-checked — **B3 flags it** (`computed ['A'] ≠ stamped ['B']`, with both perimeters and the comparison
word in the report line). The check works; the defect is simply not present in this tree. How Venkat saw a
B-keyed Q19 (an older deployed copy? the app database? a misread?) cannot be determined from this repository
and is left to the reviewer.

### Severity split

- **grades-a-correct-child-wrong: 0 found** (within the audit's reach).
- **cosmetic/other: 0 found.**

This split covers only what the audit could check: the 516 checkable questions for key accuracy, plus all
3075 for structure (B4) and enrichment consistency (B5). It says nothing about the arithmetic accuracy of
the 2,559 prose/figure-dependent keys.

## Deviations (mandatory)

1. **The brief's Q19 premise is not reproducible in this tree** — stamped key is A (correct), in source and
   on-disk review page alike; git history shows no amendment since first tracking. Reported as a finding; B3's
   ability to catch the described defect proven by in-memory re-key. No fix was made (none was needed in-tree).
2. **Construct (P4) is untestable here**: `raoGeoEngine.js` is not in the repository; `window.RaoGeo` exists
   only as a test stub in `tools/verify-reset.js:61`. Consequence beyond this audit: on-disk review pages for
   the 5 construct lessons render 'Geometry engine not loaded.' where the geometry board should be.
3. **Ruler-slide (P3) untested**: zero Grade-4 questions use it; the brief requires testing with a real lesson
   question, and none exists.
4. **sequence-build Check tap quirk (harness, not engine)**: after the sb drags, the first CDP tap on Check
   delivered pointer/touch events to the button but Chrome synthesized no `click`; a second tap (Playwright
   `page.tap()`, also real touch) fired normally. Drag steps 1–3 were unaffected. Suspected double-tap
   disambiguation in the emulation; disclosed rather than hidden. The other two paths graded on the first tap.
5. **`review/__vf_Simple fractions….html`** appeared untracked mid-session (mtime 00:49 IST): it is
   `verify-format.js`'s temp page (`tools/verify-format.js:126`), created by a concurrent process from another
   session (two unrelated `node.exe` processes were live). Not created, touched, or deleted by this audit.
6. **CHECKABLE is defined by solver success**: a question counts as checkable only when a strict-pattern solver
   actually derived its answer. This is deliberately conservative — many word problems a human could verify are
   counted NOT CHECKABLE rather than risk computing the wrong quantity and flagging a correct key.
7. **Heuristics chosen where the brief left method open**, each with its risk:
   - *Superlative options check (B3)* skips questions with figures, figure-options, money contexts, and
     'greatest number of <noun>' word problems (all were observed false-positive classes). **FN risk: a
     superlative question with a wrong key in those contexts goes unchecked.**
   - *Order sorting*: 'estimate … to the nearest N, then order' sorts by round-each-operand-then-operate (the
     lesson's own taught method; exact-value sorting would wrongly flag `estimate_differences_all` q19).
     'Digit sum' and 'remainder' sorts are computed as named. Ties → not checkable.
   - *Elapsed time*: direction decided by narrative position (clock time before all durations = start, after
     = end; mixed → not checkable). **FN risk on convoluted narratives; FP risk judged low.**
   - *B5 explain/solution checks are restricted to typed-value questions (`fill-blanks`, etc.)*: for selects,
     the key is an option LABEL (an index, an expression, a shape id) and comparing it against the explain's
     concluded quantity produced ~80 category-error false flags in the first sweep. **FN risk: a select whose
     explain genuinely contradicts its key is NOT flagged by B5.** Single-digit keys (missing-digit puzzles)
     and fraction keys are also skipped for the same reason.
   - *B5 hint check* only catches a literal 'answer is N' — hint contradictions phrased any other way are not detected.
   - *B2 figure checks* read axis-aligned `<rect>`s with exactly two nearby numeric dimension labels; the
     figure-vs-prompt contradiction check fires only in the unambiguous 1-pair/1-rect case (2 questions).
     Compound shapes, triangles, and L-shapes are NOT machine-read (counted figure-dependent).
   - *Categorize/venn* solved only when every zone label parses to a predicate (thresholds incl. units,
     divisibility, even/odd, quotient, trailing-zeros) and every tile evaluates; any figure present → skipped.
8. **Terminal print of this report is condensed** — the full per-question tables total ~2,700 rows and exceed
   the terminal tool's output limit; the on-disk file carries every row, untruncated.
9. Transient tool errors during the session: none that affected results (a Windows cp1252 console-encoding
   crash in an intermediate print was fixed by forcing UTF-8 output; a first-draft vs-tile regex bug and an
   arithmetic-regex backtracking bug were found by the triage loop and fixed — both are visible in the
   scratch scripts' history of sweeps, `tools/scratch/sweep*.txt`).
10. **Concurrent-session activity observed, disclosed for the record**: at session end `git status` reads
    'up to date with origin/main' although mid-session it read 'ahead by 6 commits' — the other live session
    pushed those commits while this audit ran. The `review/__vf_…` temp file likewise disappeared when that
    session's verify-format run finished. **This audit made zero commits and zero pushes**; `git diff` on
    tracked files is empty. Final untracked additions from this audit: `docs/audits/KEY-AUDIT-2026-07-19.md`
    and `tools/scratch/` only.
11. **No lesson parsed with errors**: `RaoPreview.build()` succeeded on all 118 files; zero error-level build
    issues surfaced in B4.

*End of report. No fixes were made, nothing was committed, and no follow-on work was self-commissioned.*
